POTUS actually gets into this a lot, saying ‚Äúin my opinion‚Äù before stating something that is objectively true or false. Ex: when he says that ‚Äúin my opinion‚Äù NYT or WaPo sources don‚Äôt exist. That‚Äôs not an opinion, that‚Äôs a claim of fact, which is a different thing.
